<span class="token keyword">import</span> instaloader
<span class="token keyword">import</span> re
<span class="token keyword">import</span> json
<span class="token keyword">from</span> datetime <span class="token keyword">import</span> datetime

<span class="token comment"># إعداد Instaloader (بدون تسجيل دخول للبيانات العامة)</span>
L <span class="token operator">=</span> instaloader<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Instaloader<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment"># الهاشتاجات المستهدفة (التشطيبات في مصر)</span>
HASHTAGS <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
    <span class="token string">'تشطيبات_مصر'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'مقاولات_القاهرة'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'ديكور_مصر'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'شقق_للتشطيب'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'تشطيب_شقق'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'مقاول_تشطيب'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'تشطيبات_داخلية'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'دهانات_شقق'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'سيراميك_مصر'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'مقاول_بناء'</span>
<span class="token punctuation">]</span>

<span class="token comment"># نمط استخراج الأرقام المصرية</span>
PHONE_PATTERN <span class="token operator">=</span> re<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">compile</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">r'(?:\+?20|0)?(1[0-5]\d{8})'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

results <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

<span class="token keyword">for</span> hashtag <span class="token keyword">in</span> HASHTAGS<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">try</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f"جاري جمع البوستات من #</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>hashtag<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">..."</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        posts <span class="token operator">=</span> instaloader<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Hashtag<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_name<span class="token punctuation">(</span>L<span class="token punctuation">.</span>context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> hashtag<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_posts<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">for</span> post <span class="token keyword">in</span> posts<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token comment"># جمع التعليقات أيضًا (أحيانًا يكون الرقم في التعليقات)</span>
            caption <span class="token operator">=</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>caption <span class="token keyword">or</span> <span class="token string">""</span>
            comments_text <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">""</span>
            
            <span class="token keyword">try</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                <span class="token keyword">for</span> comment <span class="token keyword">in</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_comments<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                    comments_text <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token string">" "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> comment<span class="token punctuation">.</span>text
            <span class="token keyword">except</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                <span class="token keyword">pass</span>
            
            full_text <span class="token operator">=</span> caption <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">" "</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> comments_text
            
            <span class="token comment"># البحث عن أرقام الهواتف</span>
            phones <span class="token operator">=</span> PHONE_PATTERN<span class="token punctuation">.</span>findall<span class="token punctuation">(</span>full_text<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> phones<span class="token punctuation">:</span>  <span class="token comment"># فقط البوستات التي تحتوي على أرقام</span>
                results<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
                    <span class="token string">'date'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>date_local<span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'%Y-%m-%d'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'platform'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token string">'Instagram'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'hashtag'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> hashtag<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'username'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>owner_username<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'url'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f"https://instagram.com/p/</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shortcode<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'text'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> full_text<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'phones'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token string">', '</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>join<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'0'</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> p <span class="token keyword">for</span> p <span class="token keyword">in</span> phones<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'likes'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>likes<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                    <span class="token string">'comments_count'</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> post<span class="token punctuation">.</span>comments
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                
    <span class="token keyword">except</span> Exception <span class="token keyword">as</span> e<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">print</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f"خطأ في #</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>hashtag<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">: </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>e<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<span class="token comment"># حفظ النتائج</span>
<span class="token keyword">with</span> <span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string-interpolation"><span class="token string">f'results_</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>datetime<span class="token punctuation">.</span>now<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>strftime<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"%Y%m%d"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">.json'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'w'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> encoding<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">'utf-8'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> f<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    json<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dump<span class="token punctuation">(</span>results<span class="token punctuation">,</span> f<span class="token punctuation">,</span> ensure_ascii<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">False</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> indent<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token string">'مقاول'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'تشطيب'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'دهان'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'سيراميك'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'بورسلين'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'جبس'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'ديكور'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'تشطيب_كامل'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'تسليم_مفتاح'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token string">'تشطيب_شقة'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'تشطيب_فيلا'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">'تشطيب_محل'</span>
<span class="token punctuation">]</span>

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">is_contractor_post</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>text<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    text_lower <span class="token operator">=</span> text<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lower<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token builtin">any</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>keyword <span class="token keyword">in</span> text_lower <span class="token keyword">for</span> keyword <span class="token keyword">in</span> CONTRACTOR_KEYWORDS<span class="token punctuation">)</span></code></pre></div></div> <div data-v-763ce8f9=""></div><h3 class="">3. تصدير تلقائي إلى Google Sheets</h3><div data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code"><div data-v-13fde6a9="" data-v-8d822fd1="" class="sticky-release" style="--sticky-header-height: 42.5px;"><div data-v-13fde6a9="" class="sticky-release-rail"><div data-v-13fde6a9="" class="sticky-release-header" style="top: 0px;"><header data-v-8d822fd1="" class="segment-code-header"><div data-v-8d822fd1="" class="segment-code-header-content"><span data-v-8d822fd1="" class="segment-code-lang">Python</span> <!----> <span data-v-868ea423="" data-v-8d822fd1=""><div data-v-1005b780="" data-v-868ea423="" class="icon-button" style="width: 32px; <span class="token keyword">from</span> google<span class="token punctuation">.</span>oauth2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>service_account <span class="token keyword">import</span> Credentials

<span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">export_to_sheets</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>data<span class="token punctuation">,</span> sheet_name<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token comment"># يحتاج إعداد Google Service Account (مجاني)</span>
    scope <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'https://spreadsheets.google.com/feeds'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
             <span class="token string">'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
    
    creds <span class="token operator">=</span> Credentials<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_service_account_file<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'credentials.json'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> scopes<span class="token operator">=</span>scope<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    client <span class="token operator">=</span> gspread<span class="token punctuation">.</span>authorize<span class="token punctuation">(</span>creds<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    sheet <span class="token operator">=</span> client<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">open</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Leads - التشطيبات'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>worksheet<span class="token punctuation">(</span>sheet_name<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    
    <span class="token comment"># إضافة البيانات</span>
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> row <span class="token keyword">in</span> data<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        sheet<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append_row<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>
            row<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'date'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

            row<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'hashtag'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> row<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'page'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">''</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            row<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'username'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
            row<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">'url'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

الكمبيوتر</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 2: ابحث عن @BotFather</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">في شريط البحث اكتب: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">BotFather</code></div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">اضغط على النتيجة الأولى (الحساب الرسمي مع علامة التوثيق ✅)</div></li></ul><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 3: اضغط "Start" أو "بدء"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 4: اضغط على الأمر <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">/newbot</code></strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">أو اكتبه في الدردشة وارسله</div></li></ul><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 5: اتبع التعليمات</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">BotFather يسألك اسم البوت → اكتب أي اسم (مثلاً: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">Leads Egypt</code>)</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">يسألك اسم المستخدم (username) → يجب أن ينتهي بـ <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">bot</code> (مثلاً: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">leads_egypt_bot</code>)</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong class="">سيُرسل لك Token</strong> (مثل: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">123456789:ABCdefGHIjklMNOpqrsTUVwxyz</code>)</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong class="">انسخه واحفظه</strong> ← هذا مفتاحك السري</div></li></ul><hr><h3 class="">المرحلة 2: الحصول على Chat ID (3 نقرات)</h3><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 1: ابحث عن @userinfobot في تليجرام</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 2: اضغط "Start"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 3: سيُرسل لك معلوماتك</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">انسخ رقم <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">Id</code> (مثل: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">123456789</code> أو <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">-1001234567890</code> للمجموعات)</div></li></ul><blockquote><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">💡 <strong class="">للقناة/المجموعة:</strong> أضف البوت إلى القناة، ثم اذهب إلى <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">https://api.telegram.org/bot&lt;TOKEN&gt;/getUpdates</code> وابحث عن <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">chat_id</code></div></blockquote><hr><h3 class="">المرحلة 3: إنشاء حساب GitHub (مجاني)</h3><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 1: افتح <a data-v-3b9ae98b="" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/" rel="noreferrer nofollow noopener">github.com</a></strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 2: اضغط "Sign up"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 3: أدخل:</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">Email</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">Password</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">Username (مثلاً: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">egypt-contractor-leads</code>)</div></li></ul><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 4: اضغط "Create account"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 5: أكد الإيميل</strong> (افتح إيميلك واضغط على رابط التأكيد)</div><hr><h3 class="">المرحلة 4: إنشاء Repository (مستودع) (5 نقرات)</h3><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 1: في GitHub، اضغط الزر الأخضر "+" (أعلى يمين)</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong class="">الخطوة 2: اختر "New repository"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 3: أدخل:</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">Repository name: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">egypt-contractor-leads</code></div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">Description: <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">Scraper for contractor leads in Egypt</code></div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto">اختر <strong>Public</strong> (مجاني تماماً)</div></li></ul><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 4: اضغط "Create repository"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong class="">الخطوة 5: اضغط "uploading an existing file"</strong></div><hr><h3 class="">المرحلة 5: رفع الملفات (5 نقرات)</h3><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 1: اضغط "Add file" → "Upload files"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 2: اسحب وأفلت أو اختر الملفات:</strong></div><ul start="1"><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">social_media_scraper_egypt.py</code> (السكريبت)</div></li><li><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">requirements.txt</code></div></li></ul><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 3: في Commit changes اكتب:</strong> <code data-v-8d822fd1="" data-v-3b9ae98b="" class="segment-code-inline">Initial upload</code></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong class="">الخطوة 4: اضغط "Commit changes"</strong></div><hr><h3 class="">المرحلة 6: إضافة GitHub Actions (التشغيل اليومي) (10 نقرات)</h3><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 1: في Repository، اضغط "Add file" → "Create new file"</strong></div><div class="paragraph" dir="auto"><strong>الخطوة 2:
